# <a name="hololens-2-release-notes"></a><span data-ttu-id="82eee-103">Notas sobre a versão do HoloLens 2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-103">HoloLens 2 release notes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-104">Para garantir que você tenha uma experiência produtiva com seus HoloLens, continuamos a lançar atualizações de recursos, bugs e segurança.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-104">To ensure you have a productive experience with your HoloLens devices, we continue to release feature, bug, and security updates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-105">Nesta página, você pode ver as novidades do HoloLens a cada mês.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-105">On this page, you can see what’s new for HoloLens each month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-106">Para obter a atualização HoloLens 2 mais recente, você pode verificar se há atualizações e [atualizar manualmente](hololens-update-hololens.md#check-for-updates-and-manually-update) ou obter a FFU (Atualização Flash Completa) para piscar seu dispositivo por meio do [Advanced Recovery Companion](hololens-recovery.md#clean-reflash-the-device).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-106">To get the latest HoloLens 2 update, you can either [check for updates and manually update](hololens-update-hololens.md#check-for-updates-and-manually-update) or get the Full Flash Update (FFU) to [flash your device via Advanced Recovery Companion](hololens-recovery.md#clean-reflash-the-device).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-107">O [download](https://aka.ms/hololens2download) é mantido atualizado e fornece o build mais recente disponível.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-107">The [download](https://aka.ms/hololens2download) is kept up to date and provides the latest generally available build.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-108">O comunicado Windows 11 recente se concentrou na versão do computador Windows.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-108">The recent Windows 11 announcement was focused on the PC version of Windows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-109">Recentemente, lançamos [](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/mixed-reality-blog/what-s-new-in-windows-holographic-version-21h1/ba-p/2337067) uma atualização principal do sistema operacional para o HoloLens 2 em maio de 2021 e estamos trabalhando em uma versão futura com base nos comentários dos clientes para essa queda.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-109">We recently launched a [major OS update](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/mixed-reality-blog/what-s-new-in-windows-holographic-version-21h1/ba-p/2337067) to HoloLens 2 in May 2021, and we are working on an upcoming release based on customer feedback for this fall.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-110">Devido a um problema conhecido agora resolvido em nosso [build 21H1](hololens-troubleshooting.md#remote-assist-video-freezes-after-20-minutes)que estava afetando os usuários do Remote Assist, pausamos temporalmente a oferta de atualizações do Windows Holographic, versão 21H1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-110">Due to a now resolved [known issue in our 21H1 build that was affecting Remote Assist users](hololens-troubleshooting.md#remote-assist-video-freezes-after-20-minutes), we temporally paused the offering of Windows Holographic, version 21H1 updates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-111">Também mudamos o build padrão do ARC (Advanced Recovery Companion) para o Windows Holographic, versão 20H2 – Atualização de junho de [2021.](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-20h2--june-2021-update)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-111">We had also changed the default Advanced Recovery Companion (ARC) build to the [Windows Holographic, version 20H2 – June 2021 Update](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-20h2--june-2021-update).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-112">O build arc agora retomará direcionando o build 21H1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-112">The ARC build will now resume targeting the 21H1 build.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-21h1---june-2021-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="82eee-113">Windows Holographic, versão 21H1 – Atualização de junho de 2021</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-113">Windows Holographic, version 21H1 - June 2021 Update</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-114">Build 20348.1007</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-114">Build 20348.1007</span></span>

### <a name="onedrive-for-work-or-school-camera-roll-upload"></a><span data-ttu-id="82eee-115">OneDrive para trabalho ou escola upload de roll de câmera</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-115">OneDrive for work or school Camera Roll upload</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-116">Adicionamos um novo recurso ao aplicativo Configurações HoloLens 2, que permite que os clientes carreguem automaticamente fotos e vídeos de realidade misturada da pasta Imagens > Camera Roll do dispositivo para a pasta OneDrive correspondente para trabalho ou escola.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-116">We've added a new feature to the HoloLens 2 Settings app, which allows customers to automatically upload mixed reality photos and videos from the device's Pictures > Camera Roll folder to the corresponding OneDrive for work or school folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-117">Esse recurso aborda uma lacuna de recursos dentro do aplicativo [OneDrive](holographic-photos-and-videos.md#share-your-mixed-reality-photos-and-videos) no HoloLens 2, que dá suporte apenas ao upload automático do Roll da Câmera para o cliente conta Microsoft pessoal (e não sua conta de trabalho ou de estudante).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-117">This feature addresses a [feature gap within the OneDrive app](holographic-photos-and-videos.md#share-your-mixed-reality-photos-and-videos) on HoloLens 2, which only supports automatic Camera Roll upload to a customer's personal Microsoft account (and not their work or school account).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-118">**Como funciona**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-118">**How it works**</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-119">Visite **Configurações > sistema > Câmera de Realidade Misturada** para habilitar o "Upload da câmera".</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-119">Visit **Settings > System > Mixed Reality Camera** to enable "Camera upload."</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-120">Ao definir esse  recurso para a posição Ativado, todas as fotos ou vídeos de realidade misturada capturados em seu dispositivo serão automaticamente na fila para upload na pasta Imagens > Do Roll da Câmera do seu OneDrive para a conta de trabalho ou de estudante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-120">By setting this feature to the **On** position, any mixed reality photos or videos captured to your device will automatically be queued for upload to the Pictures > Camera Roll folder of your OneDrive for work or school account.</span></span>
    >[!NOTE]
    ><span data-ttu-id="82eee-121">Fotos e vídeos capturados antes  da habilitação desse recurso não serão na fila para upload e ainda precisarão ser carregados manualmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-121">Photos and videos captured prior to enabling this feature *will not* be queued for upload and will still need to be manually uploaded.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-122">Uma mensagem de status na página Configurações exibirá o número de arquivos pendentes de upload (ou lerá "OneDrive está atualizado" quando todos os arquivos pendentes foram carregados).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-122">A status message on the Settings page will display the number of files pending upload (or read "OneDrive is up to date" when all pending files have been uploaded).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-123">Se você estiver preocupado com a largura de banda ou quiser "pausar" o upload por qualquer motivo, poderá alternar o recurso para a **posição** Desligado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-123">If you're concerned about bandwidth or want to "pause" upload for any reason, you can switch the feature to the **Off** position.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-124">Desabilitar temporariamente o recurso garante que a fila de upload continuará aumentando conforme você adicionar novos arquivos à pasta Roll da Câmera, mas os arquivos não serão carregados até que você reabilitar o recurso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-124">Temporarily disabling the feature ensures that the upload queue will continue to increase as you add new files to the Camera Roll folder, but files will not upload until you re-enable the feature.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-125">Os arquivos mais novos serão carregados primeiro (último a entrar, primeiro a sair).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-125">Newest files will upload first (last in, first out).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-126">Se sua OneDrive tiver problemas (por exemplo, depois que **sua** senha mudar), um botão Corrigir agora será exibido na página Configurações dados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-126">If your OneDrive account has issues (for example, after your password changes) a **Fix now** button will appear on the Settings page.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-127">Não há nenhum tamanho máximo de arquivo, mas observe que arquivos grandes levarão mais tempo para carregar (especialmente se a largura de banda de upload estiver restrita).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-127">There is no maximum file size, but note that large files will take longer to upload (especially if your upload bandwidth is constrained).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-128">Se você "pausar" ou desativar o upload enquanto um arquivo grande estiver sendo carregado, o upload parcial será preservado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-128">If you "pause" or turn off upload while a large file is being uploaded, the partial upload will be preserved.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-129">Se o upload for reabilitar dentro de várias horas após ter sido "pausado" ou desligado, o upload continuará de onde parou.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-129">If upload is re-enabled within several hours of being "paused" or turned off, the upload will continue from where it left off.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-130">No entanto, se o upload for habilitado novamente após várias horas, o upload do arquivo grande será reiniciado desde o início.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-130">However, if upload is re-enabled after several hours, the large file's upload will restart from the beginning.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-131">**Problemas conhecidos e advertências**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-131">**Known issues and caveats**</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-132">Essa configuração não tem limitação criada com base no uso de largura de banda atual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-132">This setting has no built in throttling based on current bandwidth usage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-133">Se você precisar maximizar a largura de banda para outro cenário, desligue a configuração manualmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-133">If you need to maximize bandwidth for another scenario, turn off the setting manually.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-134">Upload será pausado, mas o recurso continuará a monitorar arquivos recém-adicionados ao Camera Roll.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-134">Upload will be paused but the feature will continue to monitor newly added files to Camera Roll.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-135">Reabilitar o upload quando estiver pronto para continuar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-135">Re-enable upload when you're ready for it to continue.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-136">Esse recurso deve ser habilitado para cada conta de usuário no dispositivo e só pode carregar ativamente arquivos para o usuário conectado no momento ao dispositivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-136">This feature must be enabled for each user account on the device, and it can only actively upload files for the user who is currently signed-in to the device.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-137">Se você estiver fazendo fotos ou vídeos enquanto observa a contagem de upload na página Configurações em tempo real, observe que a contagem de arquivos pendentes pode não mudar até que o arquivo atual tenha concluído o carregamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-137">If you're taking photos or videos while watching the upload count on the Settings page in real-time, note that the pending file count may not change until the current file has completed uploading.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-138">Upload pausará se o dispositivo ficar inodor ou estiver desligado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-138">Upload will pause if your device falls asleep or is powered off.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-139">Para garantir que os uploads pendentes são concluídos, use ativamente o dispositivo até que Configurações página do Configurações leia "OneDrive está atualizado" ou ajuste as configurações de sleep **do Power &.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-139">To ensure your pending uploads complete, actively use the device until the Settings page reads "OneDrive is up to date" or adjust your **Power & sleep** settings.</span></span>
### <a name="added-support-for-some-telemetry-policies"></a><span data-ttu-id="82eee-140">Adicionado suporte para algumas políticas de telemetria</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-140">Added support for some telemetry policies</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-141">As seguintes políticas de telemetria agora têm suporte no HoloLens 2:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-141">The following telemetry policies are now supported on the HoloLens 2:</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-142">ConfigureTelemetryOptInSettingsUx</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-142">ConfigureTelemetryOptInSettingsUx</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-143">DisableDeviceDelete</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-143">DisableDeviceDelete</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-144">AllowDeviceNameInDiagnosticData</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-144">AllowDeviceNameInDiagnosticData</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-145">FeedbackHubAlwaysSaveDiagnosticsLocally</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-145">FeedbackHubAlwaysSaveDiagnosticsLocally</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-146">System\AllowTelemetry e System\ConfigureTelemetryOptInSettingsUx devem ser usados juntos para ter controle total sobre a Telemetria e o comportamento no aplicativo Configurações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-146">Both System\AllowTelemetry and System\ConfigureTelemetryOptInSettingsUx should be used together to have complete control on the Telemetry and behavior in the Settings app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-147">Melhorias e correções na atualização:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-147">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-148">Corrige a corrupção de vídeo principal com calibragem de cores.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-148">Fixes major video corruption with Color calibration.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-149">Resolve um problema em que o texto pode ser truncado no menu Energia.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-149">Addresses an issue where text might be truncated in the Power menu.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-150">Habilita o suporte para a política RequirePrivateStoreOnly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-150">Enables support for the RequirePrivateStoreOnly policy.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-159">System\AllowTelemetry e System\ConfigureTelemetryOptInSettingsUx devem ser usados juntos para ter controle total sobre a Telemetria e o comportamento no aplicativo Configurações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-159">Both System\AllowTelemetry and System\ConfigureTelemetryOptInSettingsUx should be used together to have complete control on the Telemetry and behavior in the Settings app.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-1903---june-2021-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="82eee-161">Windows Holographic, versão 1903 – Atualização de junho de 2021</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-161">Windows Holographic, version 1903 - June 2021 Update</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-21h1"></a><span data-ttu-id="82eee-166">Windows Holographic, versão 21H1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-166">Windows Holographic, version 21H1</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-167">Build 20346.1002</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-167">Build 20346.1002</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-168">Essa atualização contém recursos para dois públicos-alvo; recursos que podem ser usados por qualquer pessoa em um dispositivo pelo Usuário Final e novas opções de gerenciamento de dispositivo que podem ser configuradas por administradores de IT.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-168">This update contains features for two target audiences; features that can be used by anyone on a device by the End User, and new device management options that can be configured by IT Admins.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-169">A tabela a seguir especifica os recursos relevantes para cada público-alvo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-169">The table below specifies the features that are relevant to each audience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-170">Se você for um administrador de TI, dê uma olhada em nosso Administrador [de TI – Atualizar Lista de Verificação.](#it-admin---update-checklist)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-170">If you are an IT Admin, please take a look at our [IT Admin - Update Checklist](#it-admin---update-checklist).</span></span>
>[!IMPORTANT]
><span data-ttu-id="82eee-171">Para atualizar para esse build, HoloLens 2 dispositivos devem estar executando a atualização de fevereiro de 2021 (build 19041.1136) ou mais recente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-171">In order to update to this build, HoloLens 2 device(s) must be currently running the February 2021 update (build 19041.1136) or newer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-172">Se você não estiver vendo essa atualização de recurso disponível, atualize seu dispositivo primeiro e tente novamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-172">If you are not seeing this feature update available, please update your device first and try again.</span></span>

>[!NOTE]
><span data-ttu-id="82eee-173">Atualmente, Microsoft HoloLens 2 dá suporte a atualizações de manutenção mensais (correções de bugs e segurança) para as seguintes versões:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-173">Today, Microsoft HoloLens 2 supports monthly servicing updates (bug and security fixes) for the following releases:</span></span>
>- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-174">Windows Holographic, versão 20H2 (Build 19041.1128+)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-174">Windows Holographic, version 20H2 (Build 19041.1128+)</span></span>
>- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-175">Windows Holographic, versão 2004 (Build 19041.1103+)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-175">Windows Holographic, version 2004 (Build 19041.1103+)</span></span>
>- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-176">Windows Holographic, versão 1903 (Build 18362+)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-176">Windows Holographic, version 1903 (Build 18362+)</span></span> 
>
> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-177">Com a introdução do Windows Holographic versão 21H1, estamos descontinuando as atualizações de manutenção mensal para o **Windows Holographic versão 1903.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-177">With the introduction of Windows Holographic version 21H1, **we are discontinuing monthly servicing updates for Windows Holographic version 1903**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-178">Isso nos permite se concentrar em versões mais recentes e continuar a fornecer melhorias valiosas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-178">This enables us to focus on more recent releases and continue to deliver valuable improvements.</span></span>

### <a name="introducing-the-new-microsoft-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="82eee-243">Apresentando o novo Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-243">Introducing the new Microsoft Edge</span></span>

![animação do logotipo de Microsoft Edge herdado para o novo logotipo de Microsoft Edge](images/new-edge.gif)

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-245">o novo Microsoft Edge [adota o Chromium projeto](https://blogs.windows.com/windowsexperience/2018/12/06/microsoft-edge-making-the-web-better-through-more-open-source-collaboration/) de software livre para criar uma melhor compatibilidade para os clientes e menos fragmentação da web para desenvolvedores da web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-245">The new Microsoft Edge [adopts the Chromium open source project](https://blogs.windows.com/windowsexperience/2018/12/06/microsoft-edge-making-the-web-better-through-more-open-source-collaboration/) to create better compatibility for customers and less fragmentation of the web for web developers.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-246">esse novo Microsoft Edge substitui automaticamente Microsoft Edge herdados, que [não tem mais suporte](https://blogs.windows.com/msedgedev/2021/03/09/microsoft-edge-legacy-end-of-support/) em novas versões.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-246">This new Microsoft Edge automatically replaces legacy Microsoft Edge, which is [no longer supported](https://blogs.windows.com/msedgedev/2021/03/09/microsoft-edge-legacy-end-of-support/) in new releases.</span></span>

![nova captura de tela de Microsoft Edge](images/new-edge-ui.png)

#### <a name="launching-the-new-microsoft-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="82eee-248">Iniciando o novo Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-248">Launching the new Microsoft Edge</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-249">O novo Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-249">The new Microsoft Edge</span></span> ![novo ícone de Microsoft Edge](images/new_edge_logo.png) <span data-ttu-id="82eee-251">(representado por um ícone de espiral azul e verde) é fixado na menu Iniciar e será iniciado automaticamente quando você ativar um link da web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-251">(represented by a blue and green swirl icon) is pinned to the Start menu and will automatically launch when you activate a web link.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-252">ao iniciar pela primeira vez o novo Microsoft Edge no HoloLens 2, suas configurações e dados serão importados do Microsoft Edge herdado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-252">When you first launch the new Microsoft Edge on HoloLens 2, your settings and data will be imported from legacy Microsoft Edge.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-253">se você continuar a usar o Microsoft Edge herdado depois de iniciar o novo Microsoft Edge, esses novos dados não serão sincronizados do Microsoft Edge herdado para o novo Microsoft Edge.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-253">If you continue to use legacy Microsoft Edge after launching the new Microsoft Edge, that new data will not be synced from legacy Microsoft Edge to the new Microsoft Edge.</span></span>

#### <a name="configuring-policy-settings-for-the-new-microsoft-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="82eee-254">Definindo as configurações de política para o novo Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-254">Configuring policy settings for the new Microsoft Edge</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-255">a nova Microsoft Edge oferece aos administradores de ti um conjunto muito mais amplo de políticas de navegador no HoloLens 2 do que estavam disponíveis anteriormente com o Microsoft Edge herdado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-255">The new Microsoft Edge offers IT admins a much broader set of browser policies on HoloLens 2 than were previously available with legacy Microsoft Edge.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-256">Aqui estão alguns recursos úteis para aprender mais sobre o gerenciamento de configurações de política para o novo Microsoft Edge:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-256">Here are some helpful resources for learning more about managing policy settings for the new Microsoft Edge:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="82eee-257">definir configurações de política de Microsoft Edge com Microsoft Intune</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-257">Configure Microsoft Edge policy settings with Microsoft Intune</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/configure-edge-with-intune)
- [<span data-ttu-id="82eee-258">Versão Prévia do Microsoft Edge Microsoft Edge mapeamento de política</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-258">Microsoft Edge Legacy to Microsoft Edge policy mapping</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/microsoft-edge-policy-map-legacy-to-newedge)
- [<span data-ttu-id="82eee-259">mapeamento de política do Google Chrome para Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-259">Google Chrome to Microsoft Edge policy mapping</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/microsoft-edge-policy-map-chrome-to-newedge)
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-260">documentação completa de [Enterprise de Microsoft Edge](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-260">Full [Microsoft Edge Enterprise documentation](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/)</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-261">devido ao volume de políticas de navegador com suporte pelo novo Microsoft Edge, nossa equipe não consegue garantir que cada nova política funcione no HoloLens 2.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-261">Because of the volume of browser policies supported by the new Microsoft Edge, our team is unable to guarantee that each new policy works on HoloLens 2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-262">no entanto, testamos e confirmamos o novo Microsoft Edge equivalente de cada política de Microsoft Edge herdada anteriormente com suporte no HoloLens 2 funciona conforme o esperado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-262">However, we've tested and confirmed than the new Microsoft Edge equivalent of each legacy Microsoft Edge policy previously supported on HoloLens 2 work as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-263">consulte [Versão Prévia do Microsoft Edge para Microsoft Edge mapeamento de política](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/microsoft-edge-policy-map-legacy-to-newedge) para encontrar o novo equivalente Microsoft Edge de cada política herdada de navegador Microsoft Edge que você estava usando com o HoloLens 2.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-263">See [Microsoft Edge Legacy to Microsoft Edge policy mapping](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/microsoft-edge-policy-map-legacy-to-newedge) to find the new Microsoft Edge equivalent of each legacy Microsoft Edge browser policy you were using with HoloLens 2.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-264">há pelo menos duas novas políticas de Microsoft Edge que sabemos que *não* funcionarão com HoloLens 2:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-264">There are at least two new Microsoft Edge policies that we know *will not* work with HoloLens 2:</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="82eee-265">EnterpriseModeSiteList</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-265">EnterpriseModeSiteList</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="82eee-266">EnterpriseSiteListServiceURL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-266">EnterpriseSiteListServiceURL</span></span>

#### <a name="what-to-expect-from-the-new-microsoft-edge-on-hololens-2"></a><span data-ttu-id="82eee-267">o que esperar da nova Microsoft Edge no HoloLens 2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-267">What to expect from the new Microsoft Edge on HoloLens 2</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-268">como o novo Microsoft Edge é um aplicativo Win32 nativo com uma nova camada de adaptador UWP, permitindo que ele seja executado em dispositivos somente UWP como o HoloLens 2, alguns recursos podem não estar imediatamente disponíveis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-268">Because the new Microsoft Edge is a native Win32 app with a new UWP adapter layer allowing it to run on UWP-only devices like HoloLens 2, some features may not be immediately available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-269">Daremos suporte a novos cenários e recursos nos próximos meses, portanto, verifique este espaço para obter informações atualizadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-269">We'll be supporting new scenarios and features over the coming months, so check this space for up-to-date information.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-270">**Cenários e recursos que se espera que funcionem:**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-270">**Scenarios and features expected to work:**</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-271">Experiência de primeira execução, entrar no perfil e sincronizar</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-271">First-run experience, sign in to profile, and sync</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-272">Os sites devem renderizar e se comportar conforme o esperado</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-272">Websites should render and behave as expected</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-273">A maioria das funcionalidades do navegador (favoritos, histórico, etc.) deve funcionar conforme o esperado</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-273">Most browser functionality (Favorites, History, etc.) should work as expected</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-274">Modo escuro</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-274">Dark mode</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-275">Instalando aplicativos Web no dispositivo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-275">Installing web apps to the device</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-276">instalando extensões (informe-nos se você usar qualquer extensão que não funcione corretamente no HoloLens 2)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-276">Installing extensions (please let us know if you use any extensions that don't work properly on HoloLens 2)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-277">Exibindo e marcando um PDF</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-277">Viewing and marking up a PDF</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-278">Som espacial de uma única janela do navegador</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-278">Spatial sound from a single browser window</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-279">Atualização automática e manual do navegador</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-279">Automatic and manual updating of the browser</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-280">Salvando um PDF no menu Imprimir (usando a opção "salvar em PDF")</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-280">Saving a PDF from the Print menu (using "Save to PDF" option)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-281">Extensão do Visualizador de WebXR e 360</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-281">WebXR and 360 Viewer extension</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-282">Restauração de conteúdo para a janela correta, ao navegar por várias janelas colocadas em seu ambiente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-282">Content restoration to correct window, when browsing across multiple windows placed in your environment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-283">**Cenários e recursos que não devem funcionar:**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-283">**Scenarios and features not expected to work:**</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-284">Som espacial de várias janelas com fluxos de áudio simultâneos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-284">Spatial sound from multiple windows with simultaneous audio streams</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-285">"Vê-lo, digamos"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-285">"See it, say it"</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-286">Imprimindo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-286">Printing</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-287">**Principais problemas conhecidos do navegador:**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-287">**Top browser known issues:**</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-288">A visualização da lupa no teclado Holographic foi desabilitada para o novo Microsoft Edge.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-288">The magnifier preview in the holographic keyboard has been disabled for the new Microsoft Edge.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-289">Esperamos reabilitar esse recurso em uma atualização futura, uma vez que a ampliação esteja funcionando corretamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-289">We hope to reenable this feature in a future update, once the magnification is working correctly.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-290">O áudio pode ser reproduzido na janela do navegador incorreta se você tiver outra janela do navegador aberta e ativa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-290">Audio may play from the wrong browser window if you have another browser window open and active.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-291">Você pode contornar esse problema fechando a outra janela ativa que não deveria estar reproduzindo áudio.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-291">You can work around this issue by closing the other active window that isn't supposed to be playing audio.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-292">Ao reproduzir áudio de uma janela do navegador no [modo "Follow-me"](hololens2-basic-usage.md#follow-me-stop-following), o áudio continuará a ser reproduzido se você desabilitar o modo "Siga eu".</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-292">When playing audio from a browser window in ["Follow me" mode](hololens2-basic-usage.md#follow-me-stop-following), the audio will continue playing if you disable "Follow me" mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-293">Você pode contornar esse problema interrompendo a reprodução de áudio antes de desabilitar o modo "Follow-me" ou fechando a janela com o botão **X** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-293">You can work around this issue by stopping audio playback before disabling "Follow me" mode or by closing the window with the **X** button.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-294">interagir com o active Microsoft Edge windows pode fazer com que outras janelas de aplicativo 2d fiquem inativas inesperadamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-294">Interacting with active Microsoft Edge windows may cause other 2D app windows to go inactive unexpectedly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-295">Você pode reativar essas janelas interagindo com elas novamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-295">You can reactivate these windows by interacting with them again.</span></span>

#### <a name="microsoft-edge-insider-channels"></a><span data-ttu-id="82eee-296">Microsoft Edge Canais Insider</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-296">Microsoft Edge Insider channels</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-297">a equipe de Microsoft Edge disponibiliza três canais de visualização para o Edge insider community: Beta, Dev e canário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-297">The Microsoft Edge team makes three preview channels available to the Edge Insider community: Beta, Dev, and Canary.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-298">a instalação de um canal de visualização não desinstala a versão de lançamento do Microsoft Edge no HoloLens 2, e você pode instalar mais de um ao mesmo tempo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-298">Installing a preview channel doesn't uninstall the released version of Microsoft Edge on your HoloLens 2, and you can install more than one at the same time.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-299">visite a [home page do Microsoft Edge insider](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com) para saber mais sobre a comunidade do Edge insider.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-299">Visit the [Microsoft Edge Insider homepage](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com) to learn more about the Edge Insider community.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-300">Para saber mais sobre os diferentes canais do Edge Insider e comece, visite a [página de download do Edge Insider](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-300">To learn more about the different Edge Insider channels and get started, visit the [Edge Insider download page](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-301">Há alguns métodos disponíveis para instalar os canais Microsoft Edge Insider para HoloLens 2:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-301">There are a couple methods available for installing Microsoft Edge Insider channels to HoloLens 2:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-302">**Instalação direta no dispositivo (atualmente disponível apenas para dispositivos não planejados)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-302">**Direct install on device (currently only available to unmanaged devices)**</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="82eee-303">No seu HoloLens 2, visite a página de [download do Edge Insider](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-303">On your HoloLens 2, visit the [Edge Insider download page](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download).</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="82eee-304">Selecione o **botão Baixar HoloLens 2** para o canal do Edge Insider que você deseja instalar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-304">Select the **Download for HoloLens 2** button for the Edge Insider channel you wish to install.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="82eee-305">Iniciar o arquivo .msix baixado da fila de download do Edge ou da pasta "Downloads" do dispositivo (usando Explorador de Arquivos).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-305">Launch the downloaded .msix file from the Edge download queue or from your device's "Downloads" folder (using File Explorer).</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="82eee-306">[O instalador de aplicativo](app-deploy-app-installer.md) será lançado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-306">[App installer](app-deploy-app-installer.md) will launch.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="82eee-307">Selecione o botão **Instalar**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-307">Select the **Install** button.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="82eee-308">Após a instalação bem-sucedida, você encontrará Microsoft Edge Beta, Dev ou Canário como uma entrada separada na lista **Todos os apps** do menu Iniciar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-308">After successful install, you'll find Microsoft Edge Beta, Dev, or Canary as a separate entry in the **All apps** list of the Start menu.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-309">**Instalar por meio do pc com Windows Portal de Dispositivos [(requer](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/develop/platform-capabilities-and-apis/using-the-windows-device-portal#setting-up-hololens-to-use-windows-device-portal) que o modo de desenvolvedor seja habilitado no HoloLens 2)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-309">**Install via PC with Windows Device Portal (requires [developer mode](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/develop/platform-capabilities-and-apis/using-the-windows-device-portal#setting-up-hololens-to-use-windows-device-portal) to be enabled on HoloLens 2)**</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="82eee-310">Em seu computador, visite a página [de download do Edge Insider](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-310">On your PC, visit the [Edge Insider download page](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download).</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="82eee-311">Selecione o **botão de seta para baixo** ao lado do botão "Baixar Windows 10" para o canal do Edge Insider que você deseja instalar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-311">Select the **drop-down arrow button** next to the "Download for Windows 10" button for the Edge Insider channel you wish to install.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="82eee-312">Selecione **HoloLens 2** no menu suspenso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-312">Select **HoloLens 2** in the drop-down menu.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="82eee-313">Salve o arquivo .msix na pasta "Downloads" do computador (ou em outra pasta que você possa encontrar facilmente).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-313">Save the .msix file to the "Downloads" folder of your PC (or another folder you can easily find).</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="82eee-314">Use [Windows Portal de Dispositivos](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/develop/platform-capabilities-and-apis/using-the-windows-device-portal#installing-an-app) em seu computador para instalar o arquivo .msix baixado no HoloLens 2.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-314">Use [Windows Device Portal](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/develop/platform-capabilities-and-apis/using-the-windows-device-portal#installing-an-app) on your PC to install the downloaded .msix file on HoloLens 2.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="82eee-315">Após a instalação bem-sucedida, você encontrará Microsoft Edge Beta, Dev ou Canário como uma entrada separada na lista **Todos os apps** do menu Iniciar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-315">After successful install, you'll find Microsoft Edge Beta, Dev, or Canary as a separate entry in the **All apps** list of the Start menu.</span></span>

#### <a name="using-wdac-to-block-new-microsoft-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="82eee-316">Usando o WDAC para bloquear novos Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-316">Using WDAC to block new Microsoft Edge</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-317">Para administradores de TI que buscam atualizar a política [do WDAC](windows-defender-application-control-wdac.md) para bloquear o novo aplicativo Microsoft Edge, você precisará adicionar o seguinte à sua política.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-317">For IT Admins looking to update their [WDAC policy](windows-defender-application-control-wdac.md) to block the new Microsoft Edge app, you'll need to add the following to your policy.</span></span>

``` <Deny ID="ID_DENY_D_3_0" FriendlyName="C:\Data\Programs FileRule" PackageVersion="65535.65535.65535.65535" FileName="msedge.exe" /> ```

#### <a name="managing-endpoints-for-the-new-microsoft-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="82eee-318">Gerenciando pontos de extremidade para a nova Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-318">Managing endpoints for the new Microsoft Edge</span></span>

### <a name="install-web-apps"></a><span data-ttu-id="82eee-322">Instalar aplicativos Web</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-322">Install web apps</span></span>

### <a name="webxr-and-360-viewer"></a><span data-ttu-id="82eee-329">WebXR e Visualizador 360</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-329">WebXR and 360 Viewer</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-330">O novo Microsoft Edge inclui suporte para WebXR, que é o novo padrão para criar experiências da Web imersivas (substituindo WebVR).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-330">The new Microsoft Edge includes support for WebXR, which is the new standard for creating immersive web experiences (replacing WebVR).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-331">Muitas experiências imersivas na Web foram projetadas com VR em mente (elas substituem seu campo de exibição por um ambiente virtual), mas essas experiências também têm suporte do HoloLens 2.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-331">Many immersive web experiences were designed with VR in mind (they replace your field of view with a virtual environment), but these experiences are also supported by HoloLens 2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-332">O padrão WebXR também permite experiências da Web imersivas de realidade aumentada e misturada que usam seu ambiente físico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-332">The WebXR standard also enables augmented and mixed reality immersive web experiences that use your physical environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-333">À medida que os desenvolvedores gastam mais tempo com o WebXR, prevemos que novas experiências imersivas de realidade aumentada e misturada chegarão para que HoloLens 2 clientes experimentem!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-333">As developers spend more time with WebXR, we anticipate new augmented and mixed reality immersive experiences will arrive for HoloLens 2 customers to try!</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-334">A extensão do Visualizador 360 é criada no WebXR e é instalada automaticamente junto com o novo Microsoft Edge no HoloLens 2.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-334">The 360 Viewer extension is built on WebXR and automatically installs alongside the new Microsoft Edge on HoloLens 2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-335">Essa extensão da Web oferece a capacidade de se aprofundar em vídeos de 360 graus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-335">This web extension gives you the ability to immerse yourself in 360-degree videos.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-336">O YouTube oferece a maior seleção de 360 vídeos, portanto, incentivamos você a começar lá.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-336">YouTube offers the largest selection of 360 videos, so we encourage you to start there.</span></span>

#### <a name="how-to-use-webxr"></a><span data-ttu-id="82eee-337">Como usar o WebXR</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-337">How to use WebXR</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="82eee-338">Navegue até um site com suporte a WebXR.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-338">Navigate to a website with WebXR support.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="82eee-339">Selecione o **botão Inserir VR** no site.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-339">Select the **Enter VR** button on the website.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-340">O local e a representação visual desse botão podem variar por site, mas pode ser semelhante a:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-340">The location and visual representation of this button may vary per website, but it may look similar to:</span></span>

    ![Exemplo de botão Inserir VR](images/75px-enter-vr.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="82eee-342">Na primeira vez que você tentar iniciar uma experiência WebXR em um domínio específico, o navegador solicitará consentimento para inserir uma exibição imersiva, selecione **Permitir**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-342">The first time you try to launch a WebXR experience on a specific domain, the browser will ask for consent to enter an immersive view, select **Allow**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="82eee-343">Use [HoloLens dois gestos para](hololens2-basic-usage.md#the-hand-tracking-frame) manipular a experiência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-343">Use [HoloLens 2 gestures](hololens2-basic-usage.md#the-hand-tracking-frame) to manipulate the experience.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="82eee-344">Se a experiência não tiver um botão **Sair,** use o gesto [Iniciar](hololens2-basic-usage.md#start-gesture) para retornar para casa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-344">If the experience doesn't have an **Exit** button, use the [Start gesture](hololens2-basic-usage.md#start-gesture) to return home.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-345">**Exemplos de WebXR recomendados**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-345">**Recommended WebXR samples**</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-346">Visualizador 360 (consulte a próxima seção)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-346">360 Viewer (see next section)</span></span>
- [<span data-ttu-id="82eee-347">XR Dinos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-347">XR Dinosaurs</span></span>](https://www.xrdinosaurs.com/)
- [<span data-ttu-id="82eee-348">Barista Express</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-348">Barista Express</span></span>](https://constructarca.de/game/barista-express/)
- [<span data-ttu-id="82eee-349">WebXR Paint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-349">WebXR Paint</span></span>](https://threejs.org/examples/webxr_vr_paint.html)

#### <a name="how-to-use-360-viewer"></a><span data-ttu-id="82eee-350">Como usar o Visualizador do 360</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-350">How to use 360 Viewer</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="82eee-351">Navegue até um vídeo de 360 graus no YouTube.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-351">Navigate to a 360-degree video on YouTube.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="82eee-352">No quadro de vídeo, selecione o botão de headset de realidade misturada:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-352">In the video frame, select the mixed reality headset button:</span></span>

    ![Botão para ativar o Visualizador do 360](images/enter-360-viewer.jpg)

1. <span data-ttu-id="82eee-354">Na primeira vez que você tentar iniciar o Visualizador 360 em um domínio específico, o navegador solicitará consentimento para entrar em uma exibição imersiva.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-354">The first time you try to launch 360 Viewer on a specific domain, the browser will ask for consent to enter an immersive view.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-355">selecione **Permitir**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-355">Select **Allow**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="82eee-356">[Toque de ar](hololens2-basic-usage.md#select-using-air-tap) para abrir os controles de reprodução.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-356">[Air tap](hololens2-basic-usage.md#select-using-air-tap) to bring up the playback controls.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-357">Use [raios de](hololens2-basic-usage.md#select-using-air-tap) mão e toque de ar para reproduzir/pausar, ignorar/voltar, ativar/desativar legendas ou parar a experiência (que sai da exibição imersiva).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-357">Use [hand rays and air tap](hololens2-basic-usage.md#select-using-air-tap) to play/pause, skip forward/back, turn captions on/off, or stop the experience (which exits the immersive view).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-358">Os controles de reprodução desaparecerão após alguns segundos de inatividade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-358">The playback controls will disappear after a few seconds of inactivity.</span></span>

#### <a name="top-webxr-and-360-viewer-known-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="82eee-359">Principais problemas conhecidos do WebXR e do Visualizador 360</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-359">Top WebXR and 360 Viewer known issues</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-360">Dependendo da complexidade da experiência WebXR, a taxa de quadros pode cair ou gaguejar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-360">Depending on the complexity of the WebXR experience, the framerate may drop or stutter.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-361">O suporte para junções de mão articuladas no WebXR não está habilitado por padrão.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-361">Support for articulated hand joints in WebXR is not enabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-362">Os desenvolvedores podem `edge://flags` habilitar o suporte por meio da ative a "Entrada da Mão do WebXR".</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-362">Developers can enable support via `edge://flags` by turning on "WebXR Hand Input."</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-363">360 vídeos de sites diferentes do YouTube podem não funcionar conforme o esperado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-363">360 videos from websites other than YouTube may not work as expected.</span></span>

#### <a name="providing-feedback-on-webxr-and-360-viewer"></a><span data-ttu-id="82eee-364">Fornecendo comentários sobre o WebXR e o Visualizador 360</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-364">Providing feedback on WebXR and 360 Viewer</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-365">Compartilhe comentários e bugs com nossa equipe por meio **do recurso** Enviar Comentários na nova Microsoft Edge.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-365">Please share feedback and bugs with our team via the **Send Feedback** feature in the new Microsoft Edge.</span></span>

### <a name="new-settings-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="82eee-366">Novo Configurações aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-366">New Settings app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-367">Com esta versão, estamos introduzindo uma nova versão do Configurações aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-367">With this release, we're introducing a new version of the Settings app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-368">O novo aplicativo Configurações inclui novos recursos e configurações expandidas para o HoloLens 2 nas seguintes áreas: Som, sleep do Power &, Internet do & de rede, Aplicativos, Contas, Facilidade de Acesso e muito mais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-368">The new Settings app includes new features and expanded settings for HoloLens 2 in the following areas: Sound, Power & sleep, Network & Internet, Apps, Accounts, Ease of Access, and more.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-369">Como o novo Configurações aplicativo é diferente do aplicativo Configurações herdado, todas as janelas Configurações que você colocou anteriormente em seu ambiente serão removidas após a atualização.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-369">Because the new Settings app is distinct from the legacy Settings app, any Settings windows you previously placed around your environment will be removed upon update.</span></span>

![Home page Configurações aplicativo novo](images/new-settings-app.png)

<span data-ttu-id="82eee-371">**Novos recursos e configurações**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-371">**New features and settings**</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-372">Configurações pesquisa: pesquise as configurações Configurações página inicial usando palavras-chave ou o nome da configuração.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-372">Settings search: search for settings from the Settings homepage using keywords or the setting's name.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-373">Som > sistema:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-373">System > Sound:</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="82eee-374">Dispositivos de áudio de entrada e saída: escolha independentemente seus dispositivos de áudio de entrada e saída (por exemplo, escutar áudio por meio de fones de ouvido Bluetooth ou usar um microfone USB-C para entrada de áudio).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-374">Input and output audio devices: independently choose your input and output audio devices (for example, listen to audio via Bluetooth headphones or use a USB-C microphone for audio input).</span></span>
    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="82eee-375">Bluetooth microfones não são suportados pelo HoloLens 2.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-375">Bluetooth microphones are not supported by HoloLens 2.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="82eee-376">Volume do aplicativo: ajuste independentemente o volume de cada aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-376">App volume: independently adjust the volume of each app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-377">Consulte [por controle de volume do aplicativo](#per-app-volume-control).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-377">See [per app volume control](#per-app-volume-control).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-378">Sistema > o & sleep: escolha quando o dispositivo deve ficar em atividade após um período de inatividade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-378">System > Power & sleep: choose when the device should go to sleep after a period of inactivity.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-379">Bateria > sistema: habilita manualmente o modo economia de bateria ou definir um limite de bateria no qual o modo economia de bateria ponto é ativado automaticamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-379">System > Battery: manually enable battery saver mode or set a battery threshold at which point battery saver mode turns on automatically.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-380">Dispositivos > USB: você pode desabilitar conexões USB por padrão.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-380">Devices > USB: you can disable USB connections by default.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-381">Rede & Internet:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-381">Network & Internet:</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="82eee-382">Os adaptadores Ethernet USB-C agora aparecerão na Rede & Internet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-382">USB-C Ethernet adapters will now appear in Network & Internet.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="82eee-383">As configurações do adaptador Ethernet USB-C agora estão disponíveis, incluindo seu endereço IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-383">USB-C Ethernet adapter settings are now available, including its IP address.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="82eee-384">Agora você pode habilitar o modo avião HoloLens 2.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-384">You can now enable airplane mode on HoloLens 2.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-385">Aplicativos: você pode redefinir os aplicativos padrão usados para tipos de arquivo e link.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-385">Apps: you can reset the default apps used for file and link types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82eee-386">Para obter mais informações, [consulte Se picker de aplicativo padrão.](#default-app-picker)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-386">For more information see [Default app picker](#default-app-picker).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="82eee-387">Contas > Outros usuários: os proprietários do dispositivo podem adicionar usuários, atualizar usuários padrão para proprietários de dispositivos, fazer downgrade de proprietários de dispositivos para usuários padrão e remover usuários.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82eee-387">Accounts > Other users: device owners can add users, upgrade standard users to device owners, downgrade device owners to standard users, and remove users.</span></span>
